  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

        state: 'apple_oauth_state_0bdb27b9-7476-401d-9a5f-ee2ae26d7c15'
      });

<span id="freeTextContainer10426017768149134707"><b>From the New York Times bestselling author of <i>The Coincidence of Callie & Kayden</i> comes an emotional new story about two troubled souls sharing one all-encompassing love . . .</b><br/><br/>The dark secret Kayden has kept hidden for years is finally out. Worse, he's facing charges for battery. The only way to clear his name is for Callie to speak up-something he'll never ask her to do. In</span>
  <span id="freeText10426017768149134707" style="display:none"><b>From the New York Times bestselling author of <i>The Coincidence of Callie &amp; Kayden</i> comes an emotional new story about two troubled souls sharing one all-encompassing love . . .</b><br /><br />The dark secret Kayden has kept hidden for years is finally out. Worse, he's facing charges for battery. The only way to clear his name is for Callie to speak up-something he'll never ask her to do. Instead, he'll do whatever he must to protect her . . . even if it means letting go of the only girl he's ever loved.<br /><br />Callie knows Kayden is going back to his dark place and desperately wants to save him. But that means facing her greatest fear and admitting her own painful secrets aloud. The thought of breaking her silence terrifies her-but not as much as the thought of losing Kayden forever.<br /><br />Deep in her heart, Callie knows the time has come for her and Kayden to forget the pain of the past. With the help of her friends Seth and Luke she makes a plan to show Kayden the life they could have. But can she convince him they can make a fresh start together-or is she already too late?</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7429970729169451199">So, I'm not gonna do a big review yet, but I will say it's worth the wait. I loved this book! I loved Kayden Owens and his amazing heart! I loved Callie and her will not to give up where Kayden's concerned. They're truly a beautiful couple together. They're strong and flawed but their imperfections make them real and I loved it. I lalalalala-LOVE Luke. He's such a badass and just awesome! Seth is also an incredible character and friend. I really loved this continuation of Callie and Kayden. <br/><br/>But.</span>
  <span id="freeText7429970729169451199" style="display:none">So, I'm not gonna do a big review yet, but I will say it's worth the wait. I loved this book! I loved Kayden Owens and his amazing heart! Though it makes me more anxious to read Luke's book next!! Maybe we'll get answers there! YAY for Luke's book, I love him! Oh and I love Kayden, really. He's just....*sigh*<br /><br /><br /><br />IT HAS A COVER......LOOK AT THAT COVER. LOOK AT THAT COVER. I JUST HAD MAD COVERGASM. AHHHHHHHHHH CAN'T WAIT!!!!!!!!!!!!!!! LOVE THE COVER. <div id="review_479733999" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/479733999" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/479733999?book_show_action=true">Dec 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17147503-the-redemption-of-callie-kayden">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer479733999" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9677732642125552759"><b>5 Beautiful and Healing Stars!!!</b><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/059283b5-7d9d-4720-bb76-b0402e935102_zpsb3e0c350.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401175i/778328.jpg' alt=' photo 059283b5-7d9d-4720-bb76-b0402e935102_zpsb3e0c350.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>In ‘The Coincidence of Callie and Kayden’, Callie Lawrence was saved by Kayden Owens. Now Kayden may be the one who needs saving...<br/><br/>It’s been 7 months and 14 days since I’ve read ‘The Coincidence of Callie and Kayden’. It was easily one of my favorite books of 2012. And we all know it had one helluva cliffhanger! Well, it was worth the wait! I thought the sequel was fantastic. And it picked up right where the first book left off...<br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/14759b9a-6c11-498a-8f0a-d321807a52a4_zps1eeabec2.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401175i/778329.jpg' alt=' photo 14759b9a-6c11-498a-8f0a-d321807a52a4_zps1eeabec2.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Callie is worried about Ka</span>
  <span id="freeText9677732642125552759" style="display:none"><b>5 Beautiful and Healing Stars!!!</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/059283b5-7d9d-4720-bb76-b0402e935102_zpsb3e0c350.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401175i/778328.jpg" alt=" photo 059283b5-7d9d-4720-bb76-b0402e935102_zpsb3e0c350.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>In ‘The Coincidence of Callie and Kayden’, Callie Lawrence was saved by Kayden Owens. Now Kayden may be the one who needs saving...<br><br>It’s been 7 months and 14 days since I’ve read ‘The Coincidence of Callie and Kayden’. It was easily one of my favorite books of 2012. And we all know it had one helluva cliffhanger! Well, it was worth the wait! I thought the sequel was fantastic. And it picked up right where the first book left off...<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/14759b9a-6c11-498a-8f0a-d321807a52a4_zps1eeabec2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401175i/778329.jpg" alt=" photo 14759b9a-6c11-498a-8f0a-d321807a52a4_zps1eeabec2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Callie is worried about Kayden. After finding him the way she did, she needs to see him. Make sure he’s okay. His mother (evil) is making it very difficult. <br><br>My poor, damaged Kayden. Kayden is one of my favorite book boyfriends. Something about this guy just tugs on my heart. Kayden is stuck. He can’t tell the truth about what happens, so he lets people assume what they will. By doing that, he pushes away the people that matter most to him. He doesn’t want to burden them. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/13f34cef-1f47-423e-82b0-3cabe3e22433_zps57eb8cc6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401175i/778330.jpg" alt=" photo 13f34cef-1f47-423e-82b0-3cabe3e22433_zps57eb8cc6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>“You deserve better than this.”</b><br><br>It is a struggle for these two at the beginning of the book. Once they can get to the point where Kayden can trust Callie and open up to her, things were much better. <br><i>
  <blockquote>
    <b>“I trust you, Kayden. Even if you don’t want me to.”<br><br>I want him to me like I trust him. I owe him that much.<br>I owe him a lot<br>I owe him everything.<br><br>There is something about someone trusting you enough with their secrets that it makes it easier to trust them. It’s like they’re opening their heart and in return yours should open up to them, too.</b>
  </blockquote>
</i><br><br>The thing about Callie and Kayden that I love so much is that they both are broken. They both are tortured souls with traumatic pasts. They both have a ton of issues. Separate, they are kind of a mess. But together... together they are better. Whole. Perfect for one another. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/8b7a2b1f-d4e1-4c34-8849-9e6e3124a95e_zps783fb05d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401175i/778331.jpg" alt=" photo 8b7a2b1f-d4e1-4c34-8849-9e6e3124a95e_zps783fb05d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>I realize how perfect we are for each other and also how disastrous we could end up being. Because even though we can help each other pick up the pieces of our lives, we could also break at the same time and then nothing would be left to catch us as we crumble.</blockquote>
</b><br>The turning point is when Kayden realizes he doesn’t have to do this alone. He has people he can trust. That love him. That want to be there for him. That understand him.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/4874f7d9-7d49-4f66-844b-4ae8df30d972_zpsb50d5a73.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401175i/778332.jpg" alt=" photo 4874f7d9-7d49-4f66-844b-4ae8df30d972_zpsb50d5a73.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>All he wants is for Callie to be happy. He’s the only thing that makes her happy. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Just tell me what you need to make you happy.” She looks me in the eye with tears streaming down her cheeks. <br>“You.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>Callie and Kayden have a special bond, a connection. It’s like they were made for one another. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/2279d3d9-1759-489e-a91d-17c043d1c3a3_zps15716c5e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401175i/778333.jpg" alt=" photo 2279d3d9-1759-489e-a91d-17c043d1c3a3_zps15716c5e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>Whenever she looks at me, I swear she steals another piece of my soul. Unlike most people, she doesn’t care if it’s damaged. And once we kiss, I’m gone. The broken, soulless, empty Kayden who’s existed since the first time his father beat him no longer lives. She owns me and I want nothing more than to be with her.</blockquote>
</b><br>But to truly be able to move on and get over their past, they have to confront it. It’s a very scary thing to do. It’s one thing to confide in each other, but to get it out in the open to someone else. It’s not easy. But necessary. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“You don’t forget. You just move past it. Let go. Be who you are supposed to be instead of who they make you feel like you should be.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/CallieandKayden-future_zps3143b7da.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401176i/778334.jpg" alt=" photo CallieandKayden-future_zps3143b7da.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>They can do this. As long as they are in it together, they can do it. Move on. Confront their demons. <br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote> Okay. We can do this. Because I think we’re stronger together.” </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br>They are there for one another, but this may be something they need to do alone. <br><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/9bf74447-c18d-4419-bf5f-e49893769a4d_zpsdb049267.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401176i/778335.jpg" alt=" photo 9bf74447-c18d-4419-bf5f-e49893769a4d_zpsdb049267.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>“Thank you for saving me.”<br> “Thank you for saving me too.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br>The best things about this book: <br>~The BFF’s. Not only do I love both Callie and Kayden, but Seth and Luke are two of the best friends/supporting characters. I know we are getting a Luke book (which I am stoked about) but I’m really hoping for a Seth book as well. <br>~I love the #’s (example) #10 Face the truth and let it go. <br>~Callie is the perfect heroine. She isn’t annoying at all. She is always there for the ones she loves, and her strength. She is so strong in this book. Not only is she facing her own demons, but Kayden’s as well. She is there for him. Gets him to open up and move on. <br>~Kayden. My beautifully broken boy. <br><br>A beautiful and emotional story of love, hope, healing, freedom, moving on and learning to give and accept love. If you haven’t read this series, I highly recommend it. A solid 5 star read for me. <br><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%202/CallieandKayden-neverletmego_zps304cc655.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401176ra/778336.gif" alt=" photo CallieandKayden-neverletmego_zps304cc655.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

<div id="review_483185273" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/483185273" />
    <a title="Jodie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5886874-jodie"><img alt="Jodie" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/483185273?book_show_action=true">Dec 22, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jodie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jodie" href="/user/show/5886874-jodie">Jodie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5886874-jodie?shelf=all-time-favorite">all-time-favorite</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer483185273" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7497187689524443015">Review<br/><br/>‘I’m looking into his eyes and he’s looking into mine and I wonder if maybe it wasn’t coincidence that brought me to him that night in front of the pool house. Maybe it was fate that guided me there so I could save him and he could save me and then it could lead us here to this moment where we are both completely content and free and glad we’re alive.’<br/>- Callie, THE REDEMPTION OF CALLIE AND KAYDEN<br/><br/>If I were good in finding romantic images that resembled Callie and Kayden, I would have pasted</span>
  <span id="freeText7497187689524443015" style="display:none">Review<br><br>‘I’m looking into his eyes and he’s looking into mine and I wonder if maybe it wasn’t coincidence that brought me to him that night in front of the pool house. Maybe it was fate that guided me there so I could save him and he could save me and then it could lead us here to this moment where we are both completely content and free and glad we’re alive.’<br>- Callie, THE REDEMPTION OF CALLIE AND KAYDEN<br><br>If I were good in finding romantic images that resembled Callie and Kayden, I would have pasted my review full with it. But unfortunately, I am not good in finding those images. Le sigh<br><br>First things first, what I really liked about the COINCIDENCE SERIES is the fact that the characters seems so alive. This is a well-written story. Love it.<br><br>After reading the first book in the series THE COINCIDENCE OF CALLIE AND KAYDEN in December 2012 and realizing that the second book was due to release in February 2013, I can say that I was friggin happy because that cliffhanger was unacceptable. I repeat, unacceptable. But then we all realized that the release date had been pushed back - several times. From February 2013 to February 2014 and from February 2014 to July 30th.<br><br>Dear fellow Callie and Kayden obsessed readers, we have been waiting for a very, very, very long time for the release of the second book in the Coincidence series. Let’s say that I was depressed and frustrated that the release date of the book got pushed back many times and that I was surprised that it finally was available after coming back from a three weeks vacation. I totally forgot about THE REDEMPTION. Ok, not really ‘forgot’ the thought of it was still somewhere in my mind but it has gone to the background.<br><br>THE REDEMPTION -for short- was one hell of a roller coaster... Well maybe I am over exaggerating but…whatev’ . To be honest, I don’t remember everything from THE COINCIDENCE except for the most important parts and the fact that I fell in love with both Callie and Kayden as main characters. But there is a clear difference between THE COINCIDENCE and THE REDEMPTION. While the first book of the series was the lighter part of the story, the second books dealt with the heavier part: saving each other… or rather finding their redemption. And I preferred the first book to the second book just because of that. Though I wanted them to find their ‘freedom’, I liked reading about them together but because of the problems they had to deal with first, the time of them being together being sweet and all was pretty short and practically not enough.<br><br>My mind was pretty blank while reading THE REDEMPTION. What will happen? Where will it take place? How will the story develop or how will they find their redemption? We didn’t know. I didn’t know. I didn’t know that Kayden had it that bad. Nor did I know that Luke’s life wasn’t that easy too. And the blurb wasn’t helping at all.<br><br>But here we are and I am glad that we finally got some closure. Please note and pay attention to my emphasis on the word ‘some’, because you’ve to realize that this is not the end…YET!<br><br>original review @ moringo reviews<br><br><br>--<br><br>I can't wait.<br>And because the ''Keep Calm ...'' images are like a hype now...I have created my own<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380401694i/779985.png" width="250" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><s>28th February. We can do it, now the world did not end!</s><br><br><br>Update &lt;#insert date-blegh&gt;:<br><br>You must be kidding me.<br>Yes you are.<br>I feel cheated.<br>How come that the publication date changed at the very last minute.<br>This must be a dream - wake up -!<br><br><br><br>You know what forget it. There is not even a date yet :) Hurray.. *sarcasm dripping from every word <br><br>Ebook might be released earlier, though!<br><br>Reality sucks.<br><br>I love the teasers. I am glad we have them..but it is not helping me at all. We have got a long way to go.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer194822749924149124"><i>Received an ARC from the publisher and NetGalley in exchange for an honest review. Thank you!</i><br/><br/>I can't even begin to describe all of the emotions this book made me feel while I read it. Not to mention I couldn't put it down. This was the PERFECT sequel.<br/><br/>If you haven't read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16113791.The_Coincidence_of_Callie_and_Kayden__The_Coincidence___1_' title='The Coincidence of Callie and Kayden (The Coincidence, #1) by Jessica Sorensen' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Coincidence of Callie and Kayden</a> - then please read no further.<br/><br/>We begin book two with Kayden in the hospital and Callie is not allowed to visit him. Unable to tell the truth about what really happened, he's resigned himself t</span>
  <span id="freeText194822749924149124" style="display:none"><i>Received an ARC from the publisher and NetGalley in exchange for an honest review. Thank you!</i><br /><br />I can't even begin to describe all of the emotions this book made me feel while I read it. Not to mention I couldn't put it down. This was the PERFECT sequel.<br /><br />If you haven't read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16113791.The_Coincidence_of_Callie_and_Kayden__The_Coincidence___1_" title="The Coincidence of Callie and Kayden (The Coincidence, #1) by Jessica Sorensen" rel="nofollow noopener">The Coincidence of Callie and Kayden</a> - then please read no further.<br /><br />We begin book two with Kayden in the hospital and Callie is not allowed to visit him. Unable to tell the truth about what really happened, he's resigned himself to going back home to his parents house and keeping his pain and the truth buried. He is such a broken man that he doesn't feel worthy of Callie and her love. While trying to figure out how to deal with his demons, he pushes her away.<br /><br />Callie is also carrying around a heavy secret that has traumatized her for the past 6 years. She will have to decide if it's worth confronting her past in order to heal and have a future with Kayden. <br /><br />I just LOVE these two! I felt the horror and pain they went through and it broke my heart. They understood each other having both suffered such traumatic experiences in their lives. I wanted desperately for them to find happiness and make peace with their pasts. Their story is completely addicting. Through all of their pain and suffering, they found comfort and healing with each other and it was so beautiful. There is no major cliffhanger (THANK GOD), although the ending does leave it open for the story to continue. I saw that the author has put on Goodreads that there will be another book for Callie and Kayden and I can't wait!<br /><br />I can't express how much I love these books. They are must reads!</span>

I loved this book HARD !!! </b><br><br><b>Kayden</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400918i/777421._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>"I can't really do anything with you right now." ~ its the stupidest thing that's ever left my lips, but it needs to be said. There was something about Kayden's story that took hold of my heart from page one of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16113791.The_Coincidence_of_Callie_and_Kayden__The_Coincidence___1_" title="The Coincidence of Callie and Kayden (The Coincidence, #1) by Jessica Sorensen" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a> and never let go ! I was seeking personal redemption for him......<br><br><blockquote>I'm looking into his eyes and he's looking into mine and I wonder if it wasn't a <b>coincidence</b> that brought me to him that night in front of the pool house. Maybe it was fate that guided me there <b>so I could save him and he could save me</b> and then it could lead us here to this moment where we are both completely content and free and glad we're alive.</blockquote>.....<br><br><i><b>re·demp·tion</b><br><br>1. The act of redeeming or the condition of having been redeemed.<br>2. Recovery of something pawned or mortgaged or stolen<br>3. The payment of an obligation<br>4. Deliverance upon payment of ransom; rescue.</i><br><br> I really, really, really needed this redemption to be happening for these two broken characters. I wanted to take back the precious moments in LIFE that were stolen from them.<br><br><b>Callie</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400918i/777422.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Skittish cat turned sex-kitten......I loved how Callie evolved ! She was this mouse of a girl and then....self-discovery and healing lead to a really amazing character. I found no fault with her. i repeat.....she did not even give my Kiera nerve the tingles. Her attitude was kick-ass and although she definitely had reasons to be weak.....she was strong as all hell. Girl power. The love she had for Kayden is what helped him to heal. Callie's love definitely healed all Kayden's wounds. <br><br><i>I don't know what I'm doing and all I can hope for is the best. It's the worst feeling in the world because hope has never been that kind to me.</i>~ Callie<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400918i/777423.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I.CAN'T.DO.THIS.WITHOUT.YOU.I.CAN'T.LIVE.WITHOUT.YOU.<br><br><b>
  <i>#16 Make someone understand that you understand them no matter what it takes</i>
</b><br><br><blockquote>There's this mind-blowing moment when I realize something. Someone understands me. Callie understands me. She gets it and she's not afraid of me or what's inside of me. And while I don't understand it, I want it-I want her.</blockquote> <br><br><blockquote>Maybe if I try hard enough, we'll fall into each other and become one single person and we can share our pain instead of carrying it by ourselves.<br><br>You are the only person who I can ever feel whole with.</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400918i/777424._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>#10 FACE THE TRUTH AND LET IT GO</b><br><br>Here is about the time in the book when I lost my shit. FREEDOM. Beautiful moments of when they decided to let the truth set them free. I was having those type of random bursting into tears moments....the ones where it wakes my hubby up from a deep sleep and he thinks I'm having a seizure.....I was crying !!!! GOD sooooo beautiful. I love how they let it all go.....overcoming their fears and just let it all go............<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400918i/777425.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>You gave me good. I never had good before.</blockquote><br><br><br><b>Something Like Me by Staind</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>But every time you say you love me<br>I just have to stop and catch my breath<br>How can somebody love something like me ?<br>And every time I feel I'm falling<br>You'll be there to save me from myself<br>Little angel watching over me</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400918i/777426._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jessica Sorensen ~ the queen of slow burn. You had me at Micha ....and now Kayden...and HOLY.SHIT....now my heart just transferred to Luke. I'm greedy. Please hurry and BRING IT ! I will read anything you write....to-do list, grocery list, shit-list.....you write it ....I will read it and weep........</span>

  <span id="freeText15295437210549280412" style="display:none"><br>5 soul touching stars!<br><br><b>

</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431350i/865483._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You know when you are following a series and you left with a horrible cliffy from book 1? Thank god!!<br>what good is being alive when he feels empty inside?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431350i/865487.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Dealing with what happened to him, Kayden is in a dark place.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431350i/865488.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"Each word was a cut—a scar. On and on. Cut. Slash. Scar. Scar.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431350ra/865489.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The only person who can bring him into the light to feel the things he deserves to feel is Callie.<br><br><b>"Whenever she looks at me, I swear she steals another piece of my soul."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431350i/865490.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Callie is so strong in this book. I am amazed by her. She let's out her secrets, faces her fears for Kayden and herself.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431350i/865491.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"And what do you think will come from us telling someone?"<br><br>"Freedom.”</b><br><br>Their true strength is only seen when they are together...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380426009i/850733.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"You saved me from a lifetime of self-loathing and torture. You saved me from myself, from my past, from the painful, lonely future I’d set up for myself. Sometimes the best things are the ones that aren’t planned, the decisions made while living in the moment."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431350i/865492.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_571420553" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/571420553" />
    <a title="Catarina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina"><img alt="Catarina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514808293p2/11538033.jpg" /></a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=perfect-book-boyfriend">perfect-book-boyfriend</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=awesome-heroine">awesome-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=cat-heart-these-books">cat-heart-these-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer571420553" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16564423449224242065"><b>5 Amazing redeeming starts!! </b>	<br/><br/>I’ve waited months for this book and in the end of reading it the only thing I have to say is: Totally worth the wait!! <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/592029.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i> <b> “I wish for happiness in a world full of sorrow. “</b></i><br/><br/>After that horrible and crazy cliffhanger in the end of the first book, things aren’t looking pretty for Callie and Kayden. <br/>She doesn’t know how to help him and can’t even see him which doesn’t help with her own problems that seem to aggravate during the time Kayden’s closed in a mental facility.<br/>B</span>
  <span id="freeText16564423449224242065" style="display:none"><b>5 Amazing redeeming starts!! </b>	<br><br>I’ve waited months for this book and in the end of reading it the only thing I have to say is: Totally worth the wait!! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/592029.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> <b> “I wish for happiness in a world full of sorrow. “</b></i><br><br>After that horrible and crazy cliffhanger in the end of the first book, things aren’t looking pretty for Callie and Kayden. <br>She doesn’t know how to help him and can’t even see him which doesn’t help with her own problems that seem to aggravate during the time Kayden’s closed in a mental facility.<br>But although Kayden realizes that the only thing he truly wants is Callie, he refuses to let her get into his messed up life and head. He doesn’t think he can be saved or loved, so he pushes away everyone that is trying. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414904i/818528.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But Callie knows that even when Kayden pushes her away that’s his own way of asking for help se decides that she will not give up on him. She will save him, even when he thinks he doesn’t want to. <br>She will show him that he deserves love and happiness, even when it means her giving up her own secrets and traumas. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414904i/818529.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And Kayden, even believing that there’s no solution for him, he knows that he can’t give up on Callie. He has to protect from her past, from her ghosts and make her life bright again. If if that brightness comes from a place where he doesn’t belong in. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414904i/818530.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So not giving up on the other they will eventually find strength together to deal with their ghosts and the darkness in their pasts, so they can finally find happiness in a world where sorrow peaks in every corner.<br>And their ride is just beautiful! : ) <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398409ra/769944.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book was even more angsty and broken than the previous one. But not less achingly beautiful. <br>Although Kayden pissed me off in several moments, I could see where he was coming from and I still loved him. And I especially loved Callie, her strength really surprised in this one.<br>Luke and Seth were here too and they are their awesome selves. We find out a little more about Luke and I can’t wait to read his book! ;) <br>The parents were all awful, really, all of them. I felt like killing them every time one of them appeared. <br><br>Anyway, this was a really good reading and I’m happy that I could read their story! ;) <br>If you haven’t started on these books yet, you probably should start right now! </span>

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1168994435" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12724034468505151532"><i>
  <b>"You saved me from a lifetime of self-loathing and torture. You saved me from myself, from my pain, from the painful, lonely future I'd set up for myself."</b>
</i> <br/><br/>(Finally made a review. :D)<br/><br/>I finished this book weeks ago and I rated it 5 stars. Why? because it's simply beautiful!<br/><br/>The Redemption of Callie and Kayden is way too intense, touching, and emotional compared to the first book The Coincidence of Callie and Kayden. There is so much to love in this sequel. I really feel the emotions when both </span>
  <span id="freeText12724034468505151532" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>"You saved me from a lifetime of self-loathing and torture. You saved me from myself, from my pain, from the painful, lonely future I'd set up for myself."</b>
</i> <br /><br />(Finally made a review. :D)<br /><br />I finished this book weeks ago and I rated it 5 stars. Why? because it's simply beautiful!<br /><br />The Redemption of Callie and Kayden is way too intense, touching, and emotional compared to the first book The Coincidence of Callie and Kayden. There is so much to love in this sequel. I really feel the emotions when both Kayden and Callie experienced so much pain and struggle just to to survive and be healed from their awful situations. <br />I literally cried… especially during the <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ time when Callie finally told his family about what happened to her and what Caleb had done to her.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I don’t normally cry while reading but this totally got me. Have I known, I would have picked lots of tissues before I started it in the first place.<br /><br />The romance between Callie and Kayden also got me in my feels! Their sweetness and the way they were too comfortable around each other was totally my undoing. (Where can I find a Kayden Owens in my life??)<br /><br />I admit the start was a bit slow but halfway through it already became more and more interesting. The ending, on the other hand, was satisfying and it led towards Luke’s story—which is definitely a must-read, too!<br /><br />Rating: 5 Stars</span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/671973271?book_show_action=true">Jul 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer671973271" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer250592672501685093"><b>The Redemption of Callie and Kayden </b>was a brilliant sequel to their story! <br/><br/>The story picks up right at the horrible ending of The Coincidence of Callie and Kayden and took me on a journey of healing and love. Kayden is so broken when we first see him again and Callie is in a turmoil over what happened. These two are the perfect combination and when one is lacking strength and conviction the other steps in to bolster their resolve, confidence and courage. This romance was one of my favorites to d</span>
  <span id="freeText250592672501685093" style="display:none"><b>The Redemption of Callie and Kayden </b>was a brilliant sequel to their story! <br /><br />The story picks up right at the horrible ending of The Coincidence of Callie and Kayden and took me on a journey of healing and love. Kayden is so broken when we first see him again and Callie is in a turmoil over what happened. These two are the perfect combination and when one is lacking strength and conviction the other steps in to bolster their resolve, confidence and courage. This romance was one of my favorites to date and I loved how Callie never gave up even when she might have felt like it. There is plenty of swoon and I have so many passages highlighted in my Kindle so I can go back and glory in the memories. <br /><br />Seth and Luke are back in the story and I loved them as secondary characters. They were loyal friends lending support even though they had their own problems to deal with. <br /><br />Now I can’t wait to read Luke and Violet’s story next in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17152025.The_Destiny_of_Violet_and_Luke__The_Coincidence___3_" title="The Destiny of Violet and Luke (The Coincidence, #3) by Jessica Sorensen" rel="nofollow noopener">The Destiny of Violet and Luke</a>. They seem like a dark pair and I can’t wait to find out what’s lurking in the shadows! <br /><br />This story was beautiful, emotional and touching! Fans of Callie and Kayden will not be disappointed!<br /><br /><br />One of my favorite quotes:<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Okay,” she says with a look of ecstasy on her face, and then her eyes shut. “Whatever you want.”<br />And she means it. She would do anything for me—she already has. She gave up her secret, she gave me herself, she gave me her love. And even though I can’t tell her yet, I feel the same way about her. She owns me completely, uncontrollably, irreversibly.*<br /></i>
</b><br /><br />A copy was provided by the publisher in exchange for an honest review. Thank you!<br /><br />*Quote taken from an uncorrected proof and may change in the final copy.<br /></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer920085447" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer701176381867189206">Before diving into this, I tried to push away that gnawing voice and it's plaguing whispers of <i>it's just another cliche, IT'S JUST ANOTHER CLICHE</i> to the back of my head and carry on- and I believe it worked. Although the main issues this novel deals with have no direct relation to me, I still found myself forming a weird connection to it; my guess is it's because of how shitty parents can really be sometimes. It also kind of made me realize that I haven't got it too bad.<br/><br/>Another reason why I migh</span>
  <span id="freeText701176381867189206" style="display:none">Before diving into this, I tried to push away that gnawing voice and it's plaguing whispers of <i>it's just another cliche, IT'S JUST ANOTHER CLICHE</i> to the back of my head and carry on- and I believe it worked. Although the main issues this novel deals with have no direct relation to me, I still found myself forming a weird connection to it; my guess is it's because of how shitty parents can really be sometimes. It also kind of made me realize that I haven't got it too bad.<br /><br />Another reason why I might have liked this more than I normally would maaay just be because of this Bollywood movie I watched prior to my reading fest (it's called 2 States and yes- shitty parents strike once again!) <br /><br />Even though about 95.8% of the time, the situations that authors like to present to us through these romance stories never actually exist in real life, it's still nice to have a little hope instilled within you every now and then, right? Well, Jessica Sorensen here feeds us just that, but doesn't forget to acknowledge the fact that sometimes, some people simply aren't lucky enough to have that something or someone save them before it's too late. <br /><br />Call it overdone or whatever you want, but honestly, it feels good to read books like these once in awhile- especially when you have a bittersweet happy ending in store for you.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14574461782308234120">I was going back and forth trying to decide whether to give this book a 4 or 5. I've decided on 5 but really thinking it as:<br/><br/><b> 4.75/5 </b><br/><br/>The second installment of the <i> The Coincidence </i> series started after the major cliffhanger at the end of <i> The Coincidence of Callie and Kayden </i> where Kayden was so broken and Callie devastated from seeing him like that. Kayden is charged for battery and realizes that the only way to get out of it is for Callie to tell what had happened. Instead of making her do that</span>
  <span id="freeText14574461782308234120" style="display:none">I was going back and forth trying to decide whether to give this book a 4 or 5. I've decided on 5 but really thinking it as:<br /><br /><b> 4.75/5 </b><br /><br />The second installment of the <i> The Coincidence </i> series started after the major cliffhanger at the end of <i> The Coincidence of Callie and Kayden </i> where Kayden was so broken and Callie devastated from seeing him like that. Kayden is charged for battery and realizes that the only way to get out of it is for Callie to tell what had happened. Instead of making her do that, he is determined to protect her which means leaving her and letting her go.<br /><br />Callie knows what he is going through and wants to be there for him. To do this, she would have to dig up her past and share to everyone what had happened on her 12th birthday. She would much rather that than losing Kayden.<br /><br />With their friends help, Callie tries to make a plan to show Kayden the life they all want and deserve. She just hopes that it is enough for them to be together.<br /><br />They learn to move on from their dark pasts and heal together. Their love is even deeper from their understanding the hardships that both of them have been through.<br /><br />This quote is one that I remember sowing how much they love each other:<br /><br /><b>
  <i> "His scruffy face is like sandpaper against my skin as I clutch onto him, wanting him to touch me all over and terrified by the thought of him ever letting go. I’d latch onto him endlessly if I could, so I know he’ll be okay—we’ll be okay." </i>
</b><br /><br />I loved this book more than the last one despite the fact that there were more scenes or parts of the book that I skipped over. Seth is still very funny and I'm happy that he is also overcoming his past. I know that the third book is about Luke which is good since he is still a mystery after these two books.<br /><br />I was touched and was able to relate and understand these characters despite never going through anything remotely as difficult as that. Ms. Sorensen is obviously a very good writer who is able to write a great second book.<br /><br />I'm going to read the third book but I am definitely going to have to get used to it being about different people.</span>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9462858890395525717"><br/>After reading the first book in the series, <i>The Coincidence of Callie and Kayden</i>, I couldn’t wait to get my hands on this installment. The cliffhanger left me stunned. I was reeling from shock. And I was literally choked up. Jessica Sorenson delivers another emotional story that left me satisfied… but with mixed feelings.<br/><br/><i>The Redemption of Callie and Kayden</i> picks up where book one left off. Kayden is in the hospital after his abusive father stabbed him. Kayden is trying to recover from the trauma</span>
  <span id="freeText9462858890395525717" style="display:none"><br />After reading the first book in the series, <i>The Coincidence of Callie and Kayden</i>, I couldn’t wait to get my hands on this installment. The cliffhanger left me stunned. I was reeling from shock. And I was literally choked up. Jessica Sorenson delivers another emotional story that left me satisfied… but with mixed feelings.<br /><br /><i>The Redemption of Callie and Kayden</i> picks up where book one left off. Kayden is in the hospital after his abusive father stabbed him. Kayden is trying to recover from the trauma but feels overwhelmed and shuts out everyone, even Callie. She wants to help Kayden but feels helpless. Finding out Kayden is a cutter makes her fear for his life, yet she is too timid to confront him on it. While Callie struggles with finding a way to re-establish a connection with Kayden, he is slowly drowning in pain and despair. The way his mother treats him is cold and leaves him feeling hopeless that his life will never change. The strong bond that ties Kayden and Callie together begins to unravel as they grow apart. Kayden must find a way to release the darkness inside his head so he can move on with his life. <br /><br />There are so many questions that floated through my mind once I started this story... Can Callie and Kayden rekindle the connection they had for each other? How do you overcome the darkness left after your father stabs you? Is there hope for a better life? Does Callie finally tell her family about the rape? Will there be character growth with these characters? Jessica Sorenson does not leave us hanging. We get answers. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>“Maybe if I try hard enough, we'll fall into each other and become one single person and we can share our pain instead of carrying it by ourselves.”</b>
</i><br /><br />Callie and Kayden are really lucky to have found one another. They are wonderful together. It was nice to see Callie and Kayden finally open up to each other and unload their heavy secrets. With each other, they find comfort and understanding. They find strength in one another to share what they’ve been hiding for so many years. It will take time for them heal from it all, but now they realize that silence is no longer an option. Eventually, the fragile connection they had at the beginning of the book becomes emotionally stronger. Callie and Kayden have lived with so much pain and suffering in their lives that they are broken emotionally and that makes it really hard for them to be normal teenagers in love – which means they have a long road of healing ahead of them. <br /> <br />Jessica Sorrenson does not let up in this installment. This story is MUCH darker than the first book. There is A LOT of angst. TONS. Both characters have so much inner turmoil and it was intense. Confusion, sadness, heartbreak, guilt, anger… All war within these characters heads. But Kayden is the one suffering the most in this book. I really wanted to love this story, but I found being inside Kayden’s head at times was overwhelming. I <i>knew</i> he was suffering a kind of pain that I could never imagine, but the angst was just too much. Too heavy. It overshadowed the storyline at times. There were even times when I just put the book down to feel something other than all that angst. I really needed a hug when this story ended. <br /><br />I really enjoyed the scenes with Seth and Luke and Callie. Seth is awesome and a really good best friend to Callie. I do like that Callie finally found her backbone in this story. She showed a great amount of strength to help Kayden during his time of need. She helped him realize that picking up a razor wasn’t the only solution to his problems. Callie deserves a high five for how far she’s come.<br /><br />The next book is called <i>The Destiny of Violet and Luke</i> and I’m looking forward to reading Luke’s story. Oh, Luke. I adore him. I have a strange and shivery feeling that the secret Luke is keeping will be extremely gut-wrenching. And Violet, Callie’s roommate, definitely has some issues that have been hinted at since the first book. Both these characters are a mystery and I can’t wait to read their story.<br /><br /><i>The Redemption of Callie and Kayden</i> took me on one hell of an emotional rollercoaster ride that never let up. Not once. Their story will tug at your heartstrings repeatedly. This story may be dark and sad and painful, but the romance is sweet enough to make your heart smile. While there was some resolution in this story, there are definitely a lot of things that were not resolved. This installment may have left me with mixed feelings but I still think it’s worth reading.<br /><br />Rating: B- (3.5 stars)<br />Heat: Warm<br /><br /><br />-- <i>A <a href="http://romanticbookaffairs.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Romantic Book Affairs</a> Review</i><br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>Find us on <a href="https://twitter.com/rombookaffairs" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> and <a href="http://facebook.com/rombookaffairs" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> too!</i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="9462858890395525717" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/685020222" />
    <a title="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts"><img alt="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591195447p2/16496589.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/685020222?book_show_action=true">Aug 03, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" href="/user/show/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts">Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer685020222" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12983428190320193218"><i>
  <b>"I can't do this without you." ~ Callie </b>
</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431664i/866401._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>
  <b>"….fear owned me." ~ Callie</b>
</i> <br/><br/>After reading the Coincidence of Callie and Kayden for the first time in February, I was left reeling from the cliff hanger...aghhh!!! How could the author be so crawl and finish the book at, what felt like, the middle of a chapter? I was even a little angry, not like me at all!!! <br/><br/>Then along comes the sequel, The Redemption of Callie & Kayden and all is right in my book world again. It was so worth the wait, the anticipa</span>
  <span id="freeText12983428190320193218" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>"I can't do this without you." ~ Callie </b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431664i/866401._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>"….fear owned me." ~ Callie</b>
</i> <br><br>After reading the Coincidence of Callie and Kayden for the first time in February, I was left reeling from the cliff hanger...aghhh!!! How could the author be so crawl and finish the book at, what felt like, the middle of a chapter? I was even a little angry, not like me at all!!! <br><br>Then along comes the sequel, The Redemption of Callie &amp; Kayden and all is right in my book world again. It was so worth the wait, the anticipation; it may even have made me love the book a whole lot more in the end.<br> <br><i>The story is told beautifully from the POV of both Callie and Kayden, some of the action is repeated from both perspectives which worked perfectly in my opinion.</i><br><br><i>
  <b>♥ So, why is this book so amazing.....?</b>
</i><br> <br>Callie &amp; Kayden, two beautiful people who have led less than beautiful lives for reasons completely out of their control. The harrowing subject matter in both their cases is traumatic but dealt with so sensitively by the author. You feel their pain, their anguish, their helplessness......<b>
  <i>what was going to happen?</i>
</b> I had absolutely no clue, but I was rooting for their happy ever after, their redemption, their justice.....<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431664i/866402.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In different ways their family, who are meant to be their protectors, have let them down in a big way. Callie's family are not the perpetrators but the signs are there...she didn't feel able to talk to them; so very sad. Kayden's family, well all I can say is, there's evil in his house.....<br><br>They both face desperate situations. Broken does not even come close to explaining....<b>
  <i>it's poignant, heart breaking</i>
</b>....how could anyone survive but people do....inner strength is an amazing thing. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431664i/866403._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My heart hurt reading this book, even when the characters are happy together they have so much pain trapped inside, and there are elements in their lives that are so damaged, you wonder how they can <i>
  <b>EVER</b>
</i> be truly happy....?<br><br>They both have to face their fears, release their stories, their secrets.....let people help them, maybe <i>
  <b>then</b>
</i> they can start to heal.<br><br>We see the characters grow and mature, individually and together, again the subtlety of the writing is amazing, nothing is over played...it's perfect and always true to the characters that have been amazingly developed by this talented author.<br><br>They understand each other’s pain, they don't always know this because they both keep things hidden......they come to understand.....they become the person to each other that knows everything....sex helps both of them release their pain, it's something positive they are able to do for each other.<br> <br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"….with him, everything inside me has changed and my heart and soul aren't so shadowed anymore. ~ Callie </b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431664i/866404.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>
  <i>"I love <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[you." 3 little words; so hard for them to say but happily they both manage it by the end of this book.<br><br><b>"She owns me completely, uncontrollably, irreversibly."</b> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></i>
  <br>
  <br>
</b><i>Yes there are unanswered questions, you will know them when you read the book, but I have faith. I anticipate all my wonderings will be addressed in the author’s unique beautiful, subtle, thought provoking style in, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18166143.The_Resolution_of_Callie_and_Kayden__The_Coincidence___3_5_" title="The Resolution of Callie and Kayden (The Coincidence, #3.5) by Jessica Sorensen" rel="nofollow noopener">The Resolution of Callie and Kayden</a>. <br><br>Also I can’t wait for Luke and Violets story…….. <b><i>*excited*</i></b></i><br><br><b>♥ This book is beyond amazing, beyond incredible; it's truly stunning and captivating story telling. ♥<br><br><br><br><br></b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="12983428190320193218" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer11856333835840018389">3-3.5stars<br/><br/>Jessica Sorensen has a way with words and creates amazing characters. <b>She seems to have trouble following up amazing books though. </b><br/><br/>The Redemption of Callie and Kayden was not as terrible as The Forever of Ella and MIcah. But it wasn't all that either. Considering where we left off from the first book (which was incredible btw), this sequel seemed so anti-climactic.   <span id="freeText11856333835840018389" style="display:none">3-3.5stars<br /><br />Jessica Sorensen has a way with words and creates amazing characters. <b>She seems to have trouble following up amazing books though. </b><br /><br />The Redemption of Callie and Kayden was not as terrible as The Forever of Ella and MIcah. But it wasn't all that either. Considering where we left off from the first book (which was incredible btw), this sequel seemed so anti-climactic. It felt like it just sputtered and never really had a life of its own. <br /><br />The first 60% dragged with the two broken characters living inside their heads most of the time. Things began to happen but no explosions at all considering what they were both dealing with. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Although I did think that the moment Callie confessed her abuse to her dad was so moving and powerful. This moment here is truly a testament to Jessica's writing skills. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />And the ending, I don't know what to make of it. The external issues aren't resolved by any means. But does it end here? The next book is not even about this couple? It's certainly not that rude cliffhanger we had to live with in The Coincidence but what kind of an ending was this? </span>

<div id="review_491544577" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/491544577" />
    <a title="Cindy Ann" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2126314-cindy-ann"><img alt="Cindy Ann" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/491544577?book_show_action=true">Jan 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cindy Ann" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cindy Ann" href="/user/show/2126314-cindy-ann">Cindy Ann</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer491544577" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5863658478490106724">This wasn't a bad book but not a great one either. As with the last Jessica Sorensen book the secret of Ella and Micha there wasn't an ending but just a "see how this finishes in 2013" and leaves with a major cliffhanger. It comes down to booksellers being more specific in the description about what is a series versus a book. I just think people will get frustrated reading through an entire book to want to know the ending to get to it to find that yup, you will have to wait half a year to figure</span>
  <span id="freeText5863658478490106724" style="display:none">This wasn't a bad book but not a great one either. As with the last Jessica Sorensen book the secret of Ella and Micha there wasn't an ending but just a "see how this finishes in 2013" and leaves with a major cliffhanger. It comes down to booksellers being more specific in the description about what is a series versus a book. I just think people will get frustrated reading through an entire book to want to know the ending to get to it to find that yup, you will have to wait half a year to figure it out. Augh. Overall though this book did have good character development but could have been more in-depth for the relationships that make the characters who they are. I would recommend waiting until the next installment is available so that you can actually know the end of the book. </span>
  <a data-text-id="5863658478490106724" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_681636489" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/681636489" />
    <a title="Macha" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/19393082-macha"><img alt="Macha" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1471211039p2/19393082.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/681636489?book_show_action=true">Jul 30, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Macha" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Macha" href="/user/show/19393082-macha">Macha</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17147503-the-redemption-of-callie-kayden">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19393082-macha?shelf=i-own-the-ebook">i-own-the-ebook</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer681636489" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16574317088517172412"><b> 4.5 '’ Where the leaves go ’’ stars! </b><br/><br/>This is the book I was waiting for. After that major cliffhanger in The coincidence of Callie and Kayden… I couldn’t wait to start this one! <br/><br/>I wouldn’t say I was disappointed… It was an excellent book, but I guess I had huge expectations. I still consider the first one: My Favorite book ever in the whole wide world… This was just an ‘’ excellent ‘’ book for me… not a ‘’ OMG I want to rip my heart open ‘’ book.<br/> <br/>Callie and Kayden had their share of bad experie</span>
  <span id="freeText16574317088517172412" style="display:none"><b> 4.5 '’ Where the leaves go ’’ stars! </b><br><br>This is the book I was waiting for. After that major cliffhanger in The coincidence of Callie and Kayden… I couldn’t wait to start this one! <br><br>I wouldn’t say I was disappointed… It was an excellent book, but I guess I had huge expectations. I still consider the first one: My Favorite book ever in the whole wide world… This was just an ‘’ excellent ‘’ book for me… not a ‘’ OMG I want to rip my heart open ‘’ book.<br> <br>Callie and Kayden had their share of bad experiences…<br> <br>This book is about… suffering, breathing, believing, and overcoming. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431187i/865093.jpg" width="500" height="232" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The first book focused on healing from your past… Stoping to breathe.<br> <br>This book is focused on living for the future… Taking a step forward.<br> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431187i/865094.jpg" width="313" height="219" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This is a different kind of love story… a love that you didn’t even think you could experience. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380431187i/865095.jpg" width="500" height="313" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>A heart that was stronger than you thought you had.<br> <br>But loving is not the hard part… letting yourself be loved, when you don’t understand why someone would want to be with someone like you … is the hard part. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431187ra/865096.gif" width="500" height="255" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When you start to feel overwhelmed, when everything go wrong … it’s not the time to let go… it’s time you hold even harder!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431187ra/865097.gif" width="500" height="469" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I guess this story touches me in a deeper way… Not because it’s a story about suffering and overcoming it… but mostly because it’s about opening up.<br> <br>As a future psychologist… this means a lot to me. Especially because that’s who I want to be… that person who understands. That person who cares. That person who they can trust… with the deepest feelings they have inside. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431187ra/865098.gif" width="400" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The problem is not the emotions… the problem is not dealing with them. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431188ra/865099.gif" width="500" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Not sharing your problems doesn’t mean you don’t have any…<br><br>Being scared doesn’t mean you’re weak… <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431188ra/865100.gif" width="500" height="280" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There is always someone… <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="16574317088517172412" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>
<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_17314430'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17314430-wait-for-you"><img alt="Wait for You (Wait for You, #1)" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1363819713l/17314430._SX98_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('XlnkLDt4/DsN0jDYnzd3oz3F3Q1JwgWFd0XslLepHxUgpZwyiBlx6X6i1c2Nq6zx6QMwjxrPmJlgTvyE2/ZlSA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('nQqr0ULDvOLAXZp1KotsHhz/4aWOC9wUR2Tl4Ar6nyLj9tPP8aIxMLMtf2A4F7dMyDkMJ90GQQhQb/XwZqXlfw==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
